0574:Revit 2011 to Revit 2012 Migration Log File
0574:1. Removed regeneration option globally, since only manual is supported now
0574:2. Completely rewrote CmdNewWallLayer &ndash; needs testing!
0574:3. Fixed access to compound layer structure in CmdWallLayerVolumes
0574:4. Fixed access to compound layer structure in CmdWallLayers
0574:5. Fixed access to compound layer structure in CmdSetTagType
0574:6. In CmdSetTagType, fixed error "'Autodesk.Revit.DB.TagOrientation' does not contain a definition for 'TAG_HORIZONTAL'"
0574:fixed CmdRoomWallAdjacency to use Room.GetBoundarySegments instead of obsolete Room.Boundary
0574:7. Fixed CmdMirror and CmdMirrorListAdded to use ElementTransformUtils.MirrorElements instead of obsolete doc.Mirror
0574:8. Fixed all occurrences of 'Autodesk.Revit.DB.Reference.Element' is obsolete: Property will be removed. Use Document.GetElement(Reference) instead
0574:9. Fixed all occurrences of 'Autodesk.Revit.ApplicationServices.Application.LibraryPaths' is obsolete: Use GetLibraryPaths() and SetLibraryPaths() instead
0574:10. Fixed 'Autodesk.Revit.DB.Mullion.AsFamilyInstance' is obsolete: This property is no longer needed because Mullion now derives from FamilyInstance

1836:<"#4.1"><h1 class="new" style="font-weight: bold">API Changes
